<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：从裂隙中出现废旧列车进行突击的大技。列车不可擦弹不可防御，威力也相当高，只是作为代价展开裂隙相当的费时。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你以施法检定对范围内所有目标进行一次冲撞，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">冲撞的方向为你的方向到施法源点的方向。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若你成功，则目标每有</font><font face="宋体">1点失败数，则受到1点钝击严重伤害，且你只能只能选择击退。如果目标碰撞到间隙，则目标受到你传奇风度</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">/2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">点不可避免的物理严重伤害，然后目标从另外一个间隙中传出并继续计算击退距离。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">境符「色与空的境界」</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专业：妖术</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：无懈可击的防御弹幕，看似有缝隙，但是根本不可能接近的境界，真是耍赖的能力啊。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：只有</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你被攻击时才能使用该法术，你进行一次施法检定，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">对你进行攻击的目标进行一次反射豁免，</font><font face="宋体">DC为你检定的成功数，若目标失败，则该次攻击因</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">被扭曲的空间折射而攻击失效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个</font><font face="宋体">B级空间能力，免疫空间能力的目标无视该能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">许多人因其话题性对它兴趣满满。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：当你处于一个间隙的触及范围时你可以使用该法术，你立即传送到另外一个间隙</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个</font><font face="宋体">B级的空间</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">传送</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成功</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">完成此次传送后</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">。你可以使本回合你下一次施展的本技能树下的法术动作下降</font><font face="宋体">1级（全回合动作——整轮动作——标准动作——移动动作——迅捷动作），最低为迅捷动作。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：其实一直有一个问题，如果吧一个间隙放入另外一个间隙会发生什么。好奇的少女此时开始了这个诡异的实验。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你选择两个间隙，随后两个间隙向对方移动，最后在两个间隙中心点发生对撞，然后湮灭施法类似核弹的巨大能量。对对撞地点为中心半径你的风度</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">*1公里内所有目标（不分敌我，包括自己）造成</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">100点</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">光能混合力场严重伤害，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">所有受影响的目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">强韧豁免。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：风度</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">*</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">0米</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font><font face="宋体">1分钟</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：弹幕这种东西，射出后运动一般呈扩散趋势。在弹幕数量相同的前提下，空间范围越广，弹幕的密度也就越低，这是世间的常理。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">不过，紫的弹幕空间则与其完全相反。弹幕会和时间一起收缩，密度变高。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">弹幕并不是实战向的东西，而紫大概就凭着这种实战向的攻击与用于娱乐的弹幕之间的分界线，构筑起了一道结界。这就是弹幕结界。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你对目标发射一颗弹幕，在弹幕触碰目标之后，一道由弹幕创造的收缩结界环绕在目标周围。目标每次</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">使用</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">迅捷动作，移动动作，标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，整轮动作，全回合动作，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">则目标立即受到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">相当于</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你风度值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">/</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">点不可避免的力场严重伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">境界「永夜四重结界」</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">32</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">S</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">+</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">9</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">点妖力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：语言、姿势</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：风度</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">*</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">0米</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：黑暗永远不会消散，属于妖怪的世界，即使被遗忘也不会消失。即使外面世界的人类已经拥有了颠覆天地的力量，被欲望和野心推向世界的尽头。其心中的黑暗与恐惧也不会消失，这就是，属于妖怪的境界。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你进行一次施法检定，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本次施法检定获得</font><font face="宋体">48DP招式加值，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">然后一股黑暗的波动向目标袭击，目标承受你施法检定成功数的亵渎混合力场严重伤害</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，针对本伤害，目标无法豁免</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若目标因此受到伤害，则目标被击退伤害数</font><font face="宋体">/米，并且每被击退1米，则再受到1点纯能量严重伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标被击退的路径上每</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">穿过一个间隙，则目标被击退距离增加</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">相当于</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你的传奇风度</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">/</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">米</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">，每个间隙目标只能穿过一次</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在击退结束后，目标被垂直向上方击飞之前被击退的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">总</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">距离，目标在本次击飞中失去飞行能力并且失去免疫坠落伤害的能力，然后目标立即坠落</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">并如常</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">承受本次坠落伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">结界「客观结界」</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专业：妖术</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">32</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">S</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">+</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">9</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">点妖力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：语言、姿势</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：以你为中心。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：所有敌对目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：整个冒险世界</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：这个世界，本身就是一个巨大的结界，当其整个收缩之后，就没有东西可以遁形了。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你进行一次施法检定，并记录下成功数。之后你所处的冒险世界，从尽头处出现一层透明且巨大的结界，开始对内收缩，经过你的敌人时会将其摧毁。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你对该冒险世界内所有你认定的敌对目标造成你检定成功数</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">*2点</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">的力场</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">恶性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">伤害，目标强韧豁免。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这不需要你与目标存在视野线或者效果线，只需要你认定其为敌人即可生效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：本能力可能会对剧情造成巨大的影响，</font><font face="宋体">ST有权随时禁用本能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
